\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{autoaugment__utils_8py_source_l01146}01146\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{def\ }build\_lut(histo,\ step):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{autoaugment__utils_8py_source_l01147}01147\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ Compute\ the\ cumulative\ sum,\ shifting\ by\ step\ //\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{autoaugment__utils_8py_source_l01148}01148\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ and\ then\ normalization\ by\ step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{autoaugment__utils_8py_source_l01149}01149\ \ \ \ \ \ \ lut\ =\ (tf.cumsum(histo)\ +\ (step\ //\ 2))\ //\ step}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{autoaugment__utils_8py_source_l01154}01154\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ tf.clip\_by\_value(lut,\ 0,\ 255)}
